&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span> </span></span></p><div><ix:nonNumeric name=\"ns2:DirectorsAcknowledgeTheirResponsibilitiesUnderCompaniesAct\" contextRef=\"CY_PERIOD\"><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:  none;text-autospace:none\" xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml\"><a /><a /><span style=\"font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;  color:black\">The directors are responsible for preparing the report and the  financial statements in<a /> accordance with applicable law and  regulations.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:  none;text-autospace:none\" xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml\"><a /><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span> </span></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:  none;text-autospace:none\" xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml\"><span style=\"font-size:11.0pt;font-family:  &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\">Company law requires the directors to  prepare financial statements for each financial year.<a /> Under  that law the directors have elected to prepare the financial statements in  accordance<a /> with United Kingdom Generally Accepted  Accounting Practice (United Kingdom Accounting<a /> Standards  and applicable law). Under company law the directors must not approve the<a /> financial statements unless they are satisfied that they give  a true and fair view of the state of affairs of the company and of the profit  or loss of the company for that period.<a /> In preparing these  financial statements, the directors are required to:</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:  none;text-autospace:none\" xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:  &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span> </span></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:  11.6pt;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\" xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml\"><span style=\"font-weight: bold\"><span style=\"font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\">·</span></span><a /><span style=\"font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;  color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">   </span>select suitable  accounting policies and then apply them consistently;</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:  none;text-autospace:none\" xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:  &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span> </span></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:  11.6pt;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\" xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml\"><span style=\"font-weight: bold\"><span style=\"font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\">·</span></span><a /><span style=\"font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;  color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">   </span>make judgements and  accounting estimates that are reasonable and prudent;</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:  none;text-autospace:none\" xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:  &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span> </span></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-left:11.6pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:  -11.6pt;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:11.6pt;mso-layout-grid-align:none;  text-autospace:none\" xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml\"><span style=\"font-weight: bold\"><span style=\"font-size:10.0pt;font-family:  &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\">·</span></span><a /><span style=\"font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;  color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">   </span>state whether applicable  accounting standards have been followed, subject to any material<a /> departures disclosed and explained in the financial  statements; and</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:  none;text-autospace:none\" xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:  &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span> </span></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-left:11.6pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:  -11.6pt;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:11.6pt;mso-layout-grid-align:none;  text-autospace:none\" xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml\"><span style=\"font-weight: bold\"><span style=\"font-size:10.0pt;font-family:  &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\">·</span></span><a /><span style=\"font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;  color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">   </span>prepare the financial statements  on the going concern basis unless it is inappropriate to<a />  presume that the company will continue in business.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:  none;text-autospace:none\" xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml\"><a /><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span> </span></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:  none;text-autospace:none\" xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml\"><span style=\"font-size:11.0pt;font-family:  &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\">The directors are responsible for keeping  proper accounting records that disclose with<a /> reasonable  accuracy at any time the financial position of the company and enable them to  ensure that the financial statements comply with the Companies Act 2006. They  are also responsible for safeguarding the assets of the company and hence for  taking reasonable steps for the prevention and detection of fraud and other  irregularities.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;line-height:.5pt;mso-line-height-rule:  exactly;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\" xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml\"><a /><span style=\"font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;  color:black\"><span> </span></span></p></ix:nonNumeric></div></div><div><span style=\"font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none\"><a /><a /><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span> </span></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:11.0pt;font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\">We have audited the financial statements of Canary Wharf Investments (Three) for the year ended 31 December 2010 which comprise the Profit and Loss Account, Balance Sheet and the related Notes 1 to 15.<span style=\"mso-spacerun:yes\">  </span>The financial reporting framework that has been applied in their preparation is applicable law and United Kingdom Accounting Standards (United Kingdom Generally Accepted Accounting Practice).</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none\"><a /><span style=\"font-size: 9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span> </span></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:11.0pt;font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\">This report is made solely to the company's members, as a body, in accordance with Chapter 3<a /> of Part 16 of the Companies Act 2006.<span style=\"mso-spacerun:yes\">  </span>Our audit work has been undertaken so that we might<a /> state to the company's members those matters we are required to state to them in an<a /> auditor's report and for no other purpose.<span style=\"mso-spacerun:yes\">  </span>To the fullest extent permitted by law, we do<a /> not accept or assume responsibility to anyone other than the company and the company's<a /> members, as a body, for our audit work, for this report, or for the opinions we have formed.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none\"><a /><span style=\"font-size: 9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span> </span></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-weight: bold\"><span style=\"font-size:11.0pt; font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\">Respective responsibilities of directors and auditor</span></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none\"><a /><span style=\"font-size: 9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span> </span></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:11.0pt;font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\">As explained more fully in the Statement of Directors' Responsibilities, the directors are<a /> responsible for the preparation of the financial statements and for being satisfied that<a /> they give a true and fair view.<span style=\"mso-spacerun:yes\">  </span>Our responsibility is to audit and express an opinion on<a /> the financial statements in accordance with applicable law and International Standards on<a /> Auditing (<span>UK</span> and <span><span>Ireland</span></span>).<span style=\"mso-spacerun:yes\">  </span>Those standards require us to comply with the Auditing Practices Board's (APB's) Ethical Standards for Auditors.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none\"><a /><span style=\"font-size: 9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span> </span></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-weight: bold\"><span style=\"font-size:11.0pt; font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\">Scope of the audit of the financial statements</span></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none\"><a /><span style=\"font-size: 9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span> </span></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:11.0pt;font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\">An audit involves obtaining evidence about the amounts and disclosures in the financial<a /> statements sufficient to give reasonable assurance that the financial statements are free<a /> from material misstatement, whether caused by fraud or error.<span style=\"mso-spacerun:yes\">  </span>This includes an assessment<a /> of: whether the accounting policies are appropriate to the company's circumstances and have<a /> been consistently applied and adequately disclosed; the reasonableness of significant<a /> accounting estimates made by the directors; and the overall presentation of the financial statements.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none\"><a /><span style=\"font-size: 9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span> </span></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-weight: bold\"><span style=\"font-size:11.0pt; font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\">Opinion on financial statements</span></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none\"><a /><span style=\"font-size: 9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span> </span></span></p><div><ix:nonNumeric name=\"ns3:OpinionAuditorsOnEntity\" contextRef=\"CY_PERIOD_AUDITORS\"><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:  none;text-autospace:none\" xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml\"><span style=\"font-size:11.0pt;font-family:  &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\">In our opinion the financial statements:</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:  none;text-autospace:none\" xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:  &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span> </span></span></p><p style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:  none;text-autospace:none\"><a /><span style=\"font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span>DIRECTOR<ix:nonNumeric name=\"ns4:NameDirectorSigningAccounts\" contextRef=\"CY_PERIOD_DIRECTOR3_R_J_J_LYONS\" /></span></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;line-height:.5pt;mso-line-height-rule: exactly;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><a /><span style=\"font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; color:black\"><span> </span></span></p></div><div><span style=\"font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black;mso-ansi-language:EN-GB; mso-fareast-language:EN-GB;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA\"><br /></span></div><div class=\"Section10\"><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none\"><a /><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span> </span></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops: 23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><a /><span style=\"font-weight: bold\"><span style=\"font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\">1.</span></span><a /><span style=\"font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">     </span><span style=\"font-weight: bold\">PRINCIPAL ACCOUNTING POLICIES</span></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span> </span></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-left:23.2pt;text-align:justify;text-indent: -23.2pt;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:none; text-autospace:none\"><a /><span style=\"font-size:11.0pt; font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span>A summary of the principal accounting policies of the company, all of which have been<a /> applied consistently throughout the year and the preceding year, is set out below.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span> </span></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops: 23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><a /><span style=\"font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span><span style=\"font-weight: bold\">Accounting convention</span></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span> </span></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-left:23.2pt;text-align:justify;text-indent: -23.2pt;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:none; text-autospace:none\"><a /><span style=\"font-size:11.0pt; font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span><span><ix:nonNumeric name=\"ns4:StatementOnBasisMeasurementPreparationAccounts\" contextRef=\"CY_PERIOD\">The  financial statements have been prepared under the historical cost convention  and in accordance with applicable <span xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml\"><span>United Kingdom</span></span> accounting  standards.</ix:nonNumeric></span> The financial statements have been prepared on the going concern basis as described in the Directors' Report.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span> </span></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-left:23.2pt;text-align:justify;text-indent: -23.2pt;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:none; text-autospace:none\"><a /><span style=\"font-size:11.0pt; font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span>In accordance with the provisions of FRS 1 (Revised) the company is exempt from<a /> the requirements to prepare a cash flow statement, as it is a wholly-owned<a /> subsidiary of Canary Wharf Group plc, which has prepared a consolidated cash flow<a /> statement.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span> </span></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops: 23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><a /><span style=\"font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span><span style=\"font-weight: bold\">Turnover</span></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span> </span></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-left:23.2pt;text-align:justify;text-indent: -23.2pt;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:none; text-autospace:none\"><a /><span style=\"font-size:11.0pt; font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span><span><ix:nonNumeric name=\"ns4:TurnoverPolicy\" contextRef=\"CY_PERIOD\">Turnover  represents rents receivable net of VAT and is recognised on an accruals basis  in the period in which the rents become due.</ix:nonNumeric></span></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span> </span></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops: 23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><a /><span style=\"font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span><span style=\"font-weight: bold\">Interest receivable and interest payable</span></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span> </span></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-left:23.2pt;text-align:justify;text-indent: -23.2pt;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:none; text-autospace:none\"><a /><span style=\"font-size:11.0pt; font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span>Interest receivable and payable are recognised on an accruals basis in the period in which they fall due.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span> </span></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops: 23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><a /><span style=\"font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span><span style=\"font-weight: bold\">Dividends</span></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span> </span></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-left:23.2pt;text-align:justify;text-indent: -23.2pt;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:none; text-autospace:none\"><a /><span style=\"font-size:11.0pt; font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span>Dividend distributions to the company's shareholders are recognised in the financial statements in the period in which the dividends are paid or approved by the company's shareholders.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span> </span></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops: 23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><a /><span style=\"font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span><span style=\"font-weight: bold\">Investment properties</span></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span> </span></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-left:23.2pt;text-align:justify;text-indent: -23.2pt;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:none; text-autospace:none\"><a /><span style=\"font-size:11.0pt; font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span>Investment properties are revalued annually and in accordance with SSAP 19 (Accounting for Investment Properties) no provision is made for depreciation. This departure from the requirements of the statutory accounting rules, which requires all properties to be depreciated is, in the opinion of the directors, necessary for the accounts to show a true and fair view. Depreciation is only one of the factors reflected in the annual valuation and the amount attributable to this factor is not capable of being separately identified or quantified. Surpluses or deficits are transferred to the revaluation reserve, unless a deficit exceeds previous surpluses recognised on the same property, in which case the excess is charged to the profit and loss account.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span> </span></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops: 23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><a /><span style=\"font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span><span style=\"font-weight: bold\">Leases</span></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span> </span></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-left:23.2pt;text-align:justify;text-indent: -23.2pt;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:none; text-autospace:none\"><a /><span style=\"font-size:11.0pt; font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span>Rentals payable under operating leases are charged to the profit and loss account in the period in which the rents become due.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span> </span></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-left:23.2pt;text-align:justify;text-indent: -23.2pt;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:none; text-autospace:none\"><a /><span style=\"font-size:11.0pt; font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span>Where lease incentives, including rent free periods, are received upon entering into the lease, the benefit is recognised as an adjustment to rents payable allocated evenly over the lease term or the term to the first open market rent review if earlier.</span></p></div><div><span style=\"font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black;mso-ansi-language:EN-GB; mso-fareast-language:EN-GB;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA\"><br /></span></div><div class=\"Section11\"><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span> </span></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops: 23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><a /><span style=\"font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span><span style=\"font-weight: bold\">Trade and other debtors</span></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span> </span></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-left:23.2pt;text-align:justify;text-indent: -23.2pt;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:none; text-autospace:none\"><a /><span style=\"font-size:11.0pt; font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span>Debtors are recognised initially at fair value.<span style=\"mso-spacerun:yes\">  </span>A provision for impairment is established where there is objective evidence that the company will not be able to collect all amounts due according to the original terms of the debtor concerned.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span> </span></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops: 23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><a /><span style=\"font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span><span style=\"font-weight: bold\">Trade and other creditors</span></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span> </span></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops: 23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><a /><span style=\"font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span>Trade and other creditors are stated at cost.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span> </span></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops: 23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><a /><span style=\"font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span><span style=\"font-weight: bold\">Debt</span></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span> </span></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-left:23.2pt;text-align:justify;text-indent: -23.2pt;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:none; text-autospace:none\"><a /><span style=\"font-size:11.0pt; font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span>Debt instruments are stated initially at the amount of the net proceeds. The finance costs of such debt instruments are allocated to periods over the term of the debt at a constant rate on the carrying amount. The carrying amount is increased by the finance cost in respect of the reporting period and reduced by payments made in respect of the debt of that period. Finance costs are charged to the profit and loss account.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span> </span></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops: 23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><a /><span style=\"font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span><span style=\"font-weight: bold\">Taxation</span></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span> </span></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-left:23.2pt;text-align:justify;text-indent: -23.2pt;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:none; text-autospace:none\"><a /><span style=\"font-size:11.0pt; font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span>Current tax is provided at amounts expected to be paid or recovered using the tax rates and laws that have been enacted or substantively enacted at the balance sheet date. The company is part of a UK group for group relief purposes and accordingly may take advantage of the group relief provisions whereby current taxable profits can be offset by current tax losses arising in other companies in that group.<span style=\"mso-spacerun:yes\">  </span>The group's policy is that no payment will be made for tax losses surrendered under the group relief provisions.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span> </span></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-left:23.2pt;text-align:justify;text-indent: -23.2pt;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:none; text-autospace:none\"><a /><span style=\"font-size:11.0pt; font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span>Deferred tax assets and liabilities arise from timing differences between the recognition of gains and losses in the financial statements and their recognition in the corporation tax return.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span> </span></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-left:23.2pt;text-align:justify;text-indent: -23.2pt;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:none; text-autospace:none\"><a /><span style=\"font-size:11.0pt; font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span>Under FRS 19 deferred tax is recognised in respect of all timing differences that have originated but not reversed at the balance sheet date where transactions or events that result in an obligation to pay more tax in the future or a right to pay less tax in the future have occurred at the balance sheet date.<span style=\"mso-spacerun:yes\">  </span><span><ix:nonNumeric name=\"ns4:DescriptionReasonsWhyDeferredTaxAssetShouldBeRecognised\" contextRef=\"CY_PERIOD\">A net deferred tax asset is regarded as  recoverable and therefore recognised only when, on the basis of all available  evidence, it can be regarded as more likely than not that there will be  suitable taxable profits from which the future reversal of the underlying  timing differences can be deducted.</ix:nonNumeric></span></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span> </span></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-left:23.2pt;text-align:justify;text-indent: -23.2pt;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:none; text-autospace:none\"><a /><span style=\"font-size:11.0pt; font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span>Deferred tax is not recognised when fixed assets are revalued unless by the balance sheet date there is a binding agreement to sell the revalued assets and the gain or loss expected to arise on sale has been recognised in the financial statements.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span> </span></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-left:23.2pt;text-align:justify;text-indent: -23.2pt;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:none; text-autospace:none\"><a /><span style=\"font-size:11.0pt; font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span>Deferred tax is measured on a discounted basis to reflect the time value of money over the period between the balance sheet date and the dates on which it is estimated that the timing differences will reverse, or where the timing differences are not expected to reverse, a period not exceeding 50 years.<span style=\"mso-spacerun:yes\">  </span>Discount rates of 0.4% to 2.5% have been adopted reflecting the post-tax yield to maturity that can be obtained on government bonds with similar maturity dates and currencies to those of the deferred tax assets or liabilities.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span> </span></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;line-height:.5pt;mso-line-height-rule: exactly;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><a /><span style=\"font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; color:black\"><span> </span></span></p></div><div><span style=\"font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black;mso-ansi-language:EN-GB; mso-fareast-language:EN-GB;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA\"><br /></span></div><div class=\"Section12\"><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span> </span></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops: 23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><a /><span style=\"font-weight: bold\"><span style=\"font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\">2.</span></span><a /><span style=\"font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">     </span><span style=\"font-weight: bold\">OPERATING PROFIT</span></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span> </span></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-left:23.2pt;text-align:justify;text-indent: -23.2pt;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:none; text-autospace:none\"><a /><span style=\"font-size:11.0pt; font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span>None of the directors received any emoluments in respect of their services to the<a /> company during the year or the prior year.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span> </span></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops: 23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><a /><span style=\"font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span>No staff were employed by the company during the year or the prior year.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span> </span></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-left:23.2pt;text-align:justify;text-indent: -23.2pt;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:none; text-autospace:none\"><a /><span style=\"font-size:11.0pt; font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span>Auditors' remuneration of £500 (2009: £500) for the audit of the company has been borne<a /> by another group undertaking.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align: none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span> </span></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops: 23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><a /><span style=\"font-weight: bold\"><span style=\"font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\">3.</span></span><a /><span style=\"font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;
